var countdownTicker = (function () {
  var isCountdown = false;
  var closeBtn,
    countdownTickerContainer,
    countDownDate,
    timer,
    isCountDownClosed;
  function _setSelectors() {
    closeBtn = document.querySelector(".js-esModel-countdown-close");
    countdownTickerContainer = document.querySelector(
      ".js-esModel-countdown-ticker"
    );
    isCountDownClosed = document.cookie.indexOf("esCountDown=true") === -1;
  }
  function handleCountdown() {
    _setSelectors();
    // Set the date we're counting down to
    countDownDate = new Date("July 13, 2020 12:00:00").getTime();
    // Update the count down every 1 second
    timer = setInterval(function () {
      // Get todays date and time
      var now = new Date().getTime();
      // Find the distance between now an the count down date
      var distance = countDownDate - now;
      // Time calculations for days, hours, minutes and seconds
      var days = (Math.floor(distance / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24))).toString();
      var hours = (Math.floor(
        (distance % (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) / (1000 * 60 * 60)
      )).toString();
      var minutes = (Math.floor((distance % (1000 * 60 * 60)) / (1000 * 60))).toString();
      var seconds = (Math.floor((distance / 1000) % 60)).toString();
      // Output the result in an element with id="demo"
      var dayContainer = document.getElementById("days");
      var hoursContainer = document.getElementById("hours");
      var minutesContainer = document.getElementById("minutes");
      var secondsContainer = document.getElementById("seconds");
        if (days > 0 && dayContainer) {
            dayContainer.textContent = days;
        }
        if(hoursContainer) {
            hoursContainer.textContent = hours >= 0 ? hours : 0;
        }
        if(minutesContainer) {
            document.getElementById("minutes").textContent = minutes >= 0 ? minutes : 0;
        }
        if(secondsContainer) {
            document.getElementById("seconds").textContent = seconds;
            if (distance <= 0) {
                countdownTickerContainer.classList.remove("countdown-ticker--active");
                clearInterval(timer);
            }
        }
    }, 1000);
  }

  function trackImpression() {
    var currentDate = new Date().getTime();
    var endDate = new Date("July 15, 2020 12:00:00").getTime();
    var leftTime = endDate - currentDate;
    if (
      !countdownTickerContainer.classList.contains(
        "countdown-ticker--active"
      ) &&
      leftTime > 0
    ) {
      countdownTickerContainer.classList.add("countdown-ticker--active");
      dataLayer.push({
      event: "CWNonInteractive",
      cat: "ESCountdownTicker_d",
      act: "countdown_ticker_shown",
      lab: "MG Hector Plus"
    });
    }
  }
  function handleOnload() {
    if (isCountdown) {
      if (isCountDownClosed && countDownDate - new Date().getTime() >= 0) {
        trackImpression();
      } else if (countDownDate - new Date().getTime() < 0) {
        clearInterval(timer);
      }
    } else if (isCountDownClosed) {
      trackImpression();
    }
  }

  function handleCloseClick() {
    countdownTickerContainer.classList.remove("countdown-ticker--active");
    document.cookie = "esCountDown=true;path =/";
  }
  function registerEvents() {
    _setSelectors();
    handleOnload();
    closeBtn.addEventListener("click", handleCloseClick);
  }
  return {
    registerEvents: registerEvents,
    handleCountdown: handleCountdown
  };
})();

window.addEventListener("load", function () {
  if (document.querySelector(".js-esModel-countdown-ticker"))
    countdownTicker.registerEvents();
});
if( document.readyState !== 'loading' ) {
  if (document.querySelector("#modelCountDown"))
    countdownTicker.handleCountdown();
} else {
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
  if (document.querySelector("#modelCountDown"))
    countdownTicker.handleCountdown();
});
}

<p>Headquartered in Mumbai, Mahindra and Mahindra and has two manufacturing facilities, one in Mumbai and the other in Igatpuri, Maharashtra. The Mahindra Bolero utility vehicle is the highest selling Mahindra yet and is followed by its other stalwart, the Mahindra Scorpio. Known for their rugged build and durability, Mahindra cars are hugely popular particularly in the semi-urban and rural markets in India.</p>
<br>
<p>Mahindras Alturas G4 is its flagship model and is available with an optional 4x4 variant. Apart from this, the company sells the XUV500, XUV300, Marazzo, KUV100 NXT, TUV300, TUV300 Plus, Xylo, Verito and the NuvoSport.</p>
<br>
<p>Interestingly, Mahindra is also one of the pioneers of the electric revolution in India with the Mahindra E2O and the e-Verito developed by its electric car arm  Mahindra Electric. Mahindra also owns the celebrated global design house Pininfarina. Mahindra also caters to the lifestyle segment with the Mahindra Thar, the off-road specialist, along with its participation in national motor racing through Mahindra Adventure.</p></div><div
